    <!-- Meta Pixel Code - With Advanced Matching & external_id -->
    <script>
    !function(f,b,e,v,n,t,s)
    {if(f.fbq)return;n=f.fbq=function(){n.callMethod?
    n.callMethod.apply(n,arguments):n.queue.push(arguments)};
    if(!f._fbq)f._fbq=n;n.push=n;n.loaded=!0;n.version='2.0';
    n.queue=[];t=b.createElement(e);t.async=!0;
    t.src=v;s=b.getElementsByTagName(e)[0];
    s.parentNode.insertBefore(t,s)}(window, document,'script',
    'https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js');

    // Get or generate persistent external_id
    var externalId = localStorage.getItem('meta_external_id');
    if (!externalId) {
      externalId = 'ext_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 15);
      localStorage.setItem('meta_external_id', externalId);
    }

    // Build Advanced Matching data. We intentionally DO NOT pass stored phone
    // here because the pixel auto-attaches Advanced Matching to every PageView,
    // which caused Meta to flag >50% of PageViews as having duplicate phones
    // (the same stored phone reused across sessions/users on shared devices).
    // Email is safer (rarely shared across distinct visitors), and external_id
    // is per-browser so it cannot be flagged as duplicate PII.
    var advancedMatchingData = { external_id: externalId };
    var storedEmail = localStorage.getItem('meta_user_email');
    if (storedEmail) advancedMatchingData.em = storedEmail;

    fbq('init', '1458810709218875', advancedMatchingData, {
      autoConfig: true,
      debug: false
    });

    // Global helper to update Advanced Matching from forms.
    // Phone is stored only for use on high-intent server CAPI events (Purchase
    // etc.) — never re-sent on PageView via the browser pixel.
    window.updateMetaAdvancedMatching = function(userData) {
      if (userData.email) {
        localStorage.setItem('meta_user_email', userData.email.toLowerCase().trim());
      }
      if (userData.phone) {
        localStorage.setItem('meta_user_phone', userData.phone.replace(/\D/g, ''));
      }
    };

    fbq('set', 'autoConfig', true, '1458810709218875');
    fbq('track', 'PageView');
    </script>
    <!-- End Meta Pixel Code -->

    <script>
      if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) {
        requestIdleCallback(function() { loadMetaParamBuilder(); });
      } else {
        window.addEventListener('load', function() {
          setTimeout(loadMetaParamBuilder, 2000);
        });
      }
      function loadMetaParamBuilder() {
        var metaScript = document.createElement('script');
        metaScript.src = 'https://capi-automation.s3.us-east-2.amazonaws.com/public/client_js/capiParamBuilder/clientParamBuilder.bundle.js';
        metaScript.async = true;
        document.head.appendChild(metaScript);
        metaScript.onload = function() {
          (async () => {
            try {
              var getIpFn = async function () {
                try {
                  var response = await fetch('https://api64.ipify.org?format=text');
                  return await response.text();
                } catch (e) {
                  try {
                    var response2 = await fetch('https://api.ipify.org?format=text');
                    return await response2.text();
                  } catch (e2) {
                    return '';
                  }
                }
              };
              await clientParamBuilder.processAndCollectAllParams(window.location.href, getIpFn);
            } catch (e) {
              console.warn('Meta Parameter Builder initialization error:', e);
            }
          })();
        };
      }
    </script>
